namespace = mission_EDGERSmission

country_event = {#灼见
    id = mission_EDGERSmission.1
    title = mission_EDGERSmission.1.ct
    desc = mission_EDGERSmission.1.txt
    picture = CONQUEST_eventPicture
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = yes
    option = {
        name = EDG_ERSmission_1_option_1
        add_estate_loyalty = {
            estate = estate_church
            loyalty = -50
        }
        add_country_modifier = {
            name = new_ERS_buff_0
            duration = -1
        }
        custom_tooltip = mission_EDGERSmission_1_1_txt
        tooltip = {
            add_province_modifier = {
                name = EDG_ERS_debuff_0
                duration = -1
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {
            every_owned_province = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        religion = shiite
                        religion = sunni
                    }
                }
                add_province_modifier = {
                    name = EDG_ERS_debuff_0
                    duration = -1
                }
            }
        }
        set_estate_privilege = estate_ERS_church_Ulema_Compulsory_do_missionary_work
        set_estate_privilege = estate_ERS_church_Ulema_Spread_negative_information
        set_estate_privilege = estate_ERS_church_Ulema_Incite_military_rebellion
        set_country_flag = mission_ERSmission_1_1_flag
        hidden_effect = {
            country_event = {
                id = mission_EDGERSmission.4
                days = 120
                random = 60
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = EDG_ERSmission_1_option_2
        custom_tooltip = ERSmission_1_option_2_txt
        set_country_flag = mission_ERSmission_1_2_flag
    }
}

            amount = 1
            effect = "

                limit = {
                    religion = shiite
                }
                spawn_rebels = {
                    type = religious_rebels
                    size = 1
                }
            }
            "
        }
    }
}

country_event = {#日出
    id = mission_EDGERSmission.8
    title = mission_EDGERSmission.8.ct
    desc = mission_EDGERSmission.8.txt
    picture = CONQUEST_eventPicture
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = EDG_ERSmission_8_opinion_1
        add_stability = 6
        add_country_modifier = {
            name = EDG_ERS_buff_8
            duration = 1825
        }
        custom_tooltip = EDG_ERSmission_8_opinion_1_1_txt
        hidden_effect = {
            remove_estate_privilege = estate_ERS_church_Ulema_Compulsory_do_missionary_work
            remove_estate_privilege = estate_ERS_church_Ulema_Spread_negative_information
            remove_estate_privilege = estate_ERS_church_Ulema_Incite_military_rebellion
        }

        custom_tooltip = EDG_SPACE_TT
        custom_tooltip = EDG_mission_ERSmission_8_1_txt
        clr_country_flag = mission_ERSmission_1_1_flag
        set_country_flag = EDG_mission_ERSmission_8_1_flag

        custom_tooltip = EDG_SPACE_TT
        change_estate_land_share = {
            estate = estate_church
            share = -100
        }
        hidden_effect = {
            add_country_modifier = {
                name = EDG_ERSmission_8_opinion_1_modifier
                duration = 3650
            }
            every_owned_province = {
                limit = {
                    has_province_modifier = EDG_ERS_debuff_0
                }
                remove_province_modifier = EDG_ERS_debuff_0
            }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {#投资基础设施
    id = mission_EDGERSmission.10
    title = mission_EDGERSmission.10.ct
    desc = mission_EDGERSmission.10.txt
    picture = CONQUEST_eventPicture
    is_triggered_only = yes
    trigger = {
        religion = zoroastrian
        NOT =  {
            any_owned_province = {
                has_province_modifier = EDG_ERSmission_10_opinion_1_1_modifier
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = EDG_ERSmission_10_opinion_1
        add_years_of_income = -0.08
        custom_tooltip = EDG_ERSmission_10_opinion_1_1_txt
        tooltip = {
            add_province_modifier = {
                name = EDG_ERSmission_10_opinion_1_1_modifier
                duration = -1
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {
            random_owned_province = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        has_province_modifier = EDG_ERSmission_10_opinion_1_1_modifier
                    }
                }
                add_permanent_province_modifier = {
                    name = EDG_ERSmission_10_opinion_1_1_modifier
                    duration = -1
                }
            }
            change_variable = {
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_54_opinion_1_1_var
				value = 1
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = EDG_ERSmission_10_opinion_2
        add_years_of_income = 0.15
        hidden_effect = {
            change_variable = {
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_54_opinion_1_2_var
				value = 1
            }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {#亚述斯坦复兴
    id = mission_EDGERSmission.22
    title = mission_EDGERSmission.22.ct
    desc = mission_EDGERSmission.22.txt
    picture = UNIVERSITY_eventPicture
    trigger = {
        religion = zoroastrian
        OR = {
            has_reform = EDG_new_ERS_new_Tianze_Monarchy_reforms
            has_reform = EDG_new_TAB_government_reforms
        }
        basra_area = {
            type = all
            num_of_times_improved = 2
			country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
        }
        iraq_arabi_area = {
            type = all
            num_of_times_improved = 2
			country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
        }
    }
    fire_only_once = yes
    option = {
        name = EDG_ERSmission_22_opinion_1
        custom_tooltip = EDG_ERSmission_22_opinion_1_1_txt
        hidden_effect = {
            every_owned_province = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        area = iraq_arabi_area
                        area = basra_area
                    }
                }

country_event = {#随机发展度增长
    id = mission_EDGERSmission.79
    is_triggered_only = yes
    hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_country_flag = mission_EDGERSmission_112_opinion_1_3_flag
                }
                set_variable = {
                    which = mission_EDGERSmission_112_opinion_1_3_flag_1_var
                    value = 10
                }
                while = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = {
                            which = mission_EDGERSmission_112_opinion_1_3_flag_1_var
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }
                    subtract_variable = {
                        which = mission_EDGERSmission_112_opinion_1_3_flag_1_var
                        value = 1
                    }
                    random_owned_province = {
                        limit = {
                            NOT = {
                                has_province_modifier = EDG_ERS_mission_EDGERSmission_79_1_modifier
                            }
                        }
                        add_base_tax = 1
                        add_province_modifier = {
                            name = EDG_ERS_mission_EDGERSmission_79_1_modifier
                            duration = 365
                        }
                    }
                }
                set_variable = {
                    which = mission_EDGERSmission_112_opinion_1_3_flag_2_var
                    value = 10
                }
                while = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = {
                            which = mission_EDGERSmission_112_opinion_1_3_flag_2_var
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }
                    subtract_variable = {
                        which = mission_EDGERSmission_112_opinion_1_3_flag_2_var

                            duration = 365
                        }
                    }
                }

                    value = 10
                }
                while = {

country_event = { #出售丝绸
    id = mission_EDGERSmission.133
    title = mission_EDGERSmission.133.ct
    desc = mission_EDGERSmission.133.txt
    picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
    is_triggered_only = yes
    immediate = {
        event_target:EDG_ERS_E_purchaser = {
            set_variable = { #把自己的丝绸数量传给指定国家一
                which = EDG_ERS_Purchase_silk #自己的丝绸变量
                which = prev #传递给指定国家
            }
            set_variable = { #把自己的的丝绸数量传给指定国家二
                which = EDG_ERS_Purchase_silk_copy #传递过去的丝绸数量
                which = EDG_ERS_Purchase_silk #复制丝绸数量
            }
            export_to_variable = { #创建年收入赋值
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #指定国家年收入的赋值
                value = years_of_income #取值年收入
            }
            export_to_variable = { #设置西方国库的变量
                which = EDG_ERS_E_treasury #指定国家国库的赋值
                value = trigger_value:treasury #取值国库
            }
            multiply_variable = { #将年收入乘以丝绸数量    
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
                which = EDG_ERS_Purchase_silk_copy #丝绸数量的复制变量
            }
            set_variable = { #创建年收入乘丝绸数量变量
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_silk #创建新的年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #原年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
            }
            multiply_variable = { #将乘以了丝绸变量的西方年收入乘0.7进行下一步       
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_silk
                value = 0.7
            }
            set_variable = { #最终收入
                which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_silk
            }
        }
	}
    option = {
        name = mission_EDGERSmission_133_1 #出售丝绸
        trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                which = EDG_ERS_Purchase_silk
                value = 1
            }
        }
        custom_tooltip = mission_EDGERSmission_133_1_txt
        hidden_effect = {
            event_target:EDG_ERS_E_purchaser = {
                country_event = {
                    id = mission_EDGERSmission.134
                }
            }
        }
        ai_chance = { 
            factor = 100
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = mission_EDGERSmission_133_2
        ai_chance = { 
            factor = 0
        }
    }
}
country_event = { #出售丝绸
    id = mission_EDGERSmission.134
    title = mission_EDGERSmission.134.ct
    desc = mission_EDGERSmission.134.txt
    picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = mission_EDGERSmission_134_1
        hidden_effect = {
            event_target:EDG_ERS_E_purchaser = {
                set_variable = {
                    which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury_copy
                    which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                }
                while = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = {
                            which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury_copy
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }
                    subtract_variable = { #将西方的国库减去西方乘了0.7的年收入的资金但不超过上限          
                        which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury_copy
                        value = 1
                    }
                    add_treasury = -1
                }
                event_target:EDG_ERS_Acquirer = {
                    set_variable = {
                        which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                        which = prev
                    }
                    while = {
                        limit = {
                            check_variable = {
                                which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                                value = 1
                            }
                        }
                        subtract_variable = { #将西方的国库减去西方乘了0.7的年收入的资金但不超过上限          
                            which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                            value = 1
                        }
                        add_treasury = 1
                    }
                    set_variable = {
                        which = EDG_ERS_Purchase_silk
                        value = 0
                    }
                }
            }
            ai_chance = { 
                factor = 100
            }
        }
        option = {
            name = mission_EDGERSmission_134_2
            event_target:EDG_ERS_E_purchaser = {
                set_variable = {
                    which = EDG_ERS_Purchase_silk
                    value = 0
                }
            }
            ai_chance = { 
                factor = 0
            }
        }
    }
}
country_event = { #出售香料
    id = mission_EDGERSmission.135
    title = mission_EDGERSmission.135.ct
    desc = mission_EDGERSmission.135.txt
    picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
    is_triggered_only = yes
    immediate = {
        event_target:EDG_ERS_E_purchaser = {
            set_variable = { 
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var 
                which = prev #传递给指定国家
            }
            set_variable = { 
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var_copy 
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var 
            }
            export_to_variable = { #创建年收入赋值
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #指定国家年收入的赋值
                value = years_of_income #取值年收入
            }
            export_to_variable = { #设置西方国库的变量
                which = EDG_ERS_E_treasury #指定国家国库的赋值
                value = trigger_value:treasury #取值国库
            }
            multiply_variable = { #将年收入乘以丝绸数量    
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var_copy #丝绸数量的复制变量
            }
            set_variable = { #创建年收入乘丝绸数量变量
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var #创建新的年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #原年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
            }
            multiply_variable = { #将乘以了丝绸变量的西方年收入乘0.7进行下一步       
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var
                value = 0.9
            }
            set_variable = { #最终收入
                which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var
            }
        }
	}
    option = {
        name = mission_EDGERSmission_135_1 
        trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var
                value = 1
            }
        }
        custom_tooltip = mission_EDGERSmission_135_1_txt
        hidden_effect = {
            event_target:EDG_ERS_E_purchaser = {
                country_event = {
                    id = mission_EDGERSmission.151
                }
            }
        }
        ai_chance = { 
            factor = 100
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = mission_EDGERSmission_133_2
        ai_chance = { 
            factor = 0
        }
    }
}

            multiply_variable = { #将年收入乘以丝绸数量    
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_82_3_var_copy #丝绸数量的复制变量
            }
            set_variable = { #创建年收入乘丝绸数量变量
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_mission_EDGERSmission_82_3_var #创建新的年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #原年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
            }
            multiply_variable = { #将乘以了丝绸变量的西方年收入乘0.7进行下一步       
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_mission_EDGERSmission_82_3_var
                value = 0.4
            }
            set_variable = { #最终收入
                which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_mission_EDGERSmission_82_3_var
            }
        }
	}
    option = {
        name = mission_EDGERSmission_136_1 
        trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_82_3_var
                value = 1
            }

                which = mission_EDGERSmission_132_1_var
                which = prev #传递给指定国家
            }
            set_variable = { 
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_132_1_var_copy 
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_132_1_var
            }
            export_to_variable = { #创建年收入赋值
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #指定国家年收入的赋值
                value = years_of_income #取值年收入
            }
            export_to_variable = { #设置西方国库的变量
                which = EDG_ERS_E_treasury #指定国家国库的赋值
                value = trigger_value:treasury #取值国库
            }
            multiply_variable = { #将年收入乘以丝绸数量    
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_132_1_var_copy #丝绸数量的复制变量
            }
            set_variable = { #创建年收入乘丝绸数量变量
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_mission_EDGERSmission_132_1_var #创建新的年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income #原年收入乘以丝绸数量的赋值
            }
            multiply_variable = { #将乘以了丝绸变量的西方年收入乘0.7进行下一步       
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_mission_EDGERSmission_132_1_var
                value = 1
            }
            set_variable = { #最终收入
                which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                which = EDG_ERS_E_years_of_income_mission_EDGERSmission_132_1_var
            }
        }
	}
    option = {
        name = mission_EDGERSmission_145_1 
        trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                which = mission_EDGERSmission_132_1_var
                value = 1
            }
        }
        custom_tooltip = mission_EDGERSmission_145_1_txt
        hidden_effect = {
            event_target:EDG_ERS_A_purchaser = {

                    id = mission_EDGERSmission.161

country_event = { #出售香料
    id = mission_EDGERSmission.151
    title = mission_EDGERSmission.151.ct
    desc = mission_EDGERSmission.151.txt
    picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = mission_EDGERSmission_151_1
        hidden_effect = {
            event_target:EDG_ERS_E_purchaser = {
                set_variable = {
                    which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury_copy
                    which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                }
                while = {
                    limit = {
                        check_variable = {
                            which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury_copy
                            value = 1
                        }
                    }
                    subtract_variable = { #将西方的国库减去西方乘了0.7的年收入的资金但不超过上限          
                        which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury_copy
                        value = 1
                    }
                    add_treasury = -1
                }
                event_target:EDG_ERS_Acquirer = {
                    set_variable = {
                        which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                        which = prev
                    }
                    while = {
                        limit = {
                            check_variable = {
                                which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                                value = 1
                            }
                        }
                        subtract_variable = { #将西方的国库减去西方乘了0.7的年收入的资金但不超过上限          
                            which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                            value = 1
                        }
                        add_treasury = 1
                    }
                    set_variable = {
                        which = mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var
                        value = 0
                    }
                }
            }
            ai_chance = { 
                factor = 100
            }
        }
        option = {
            name = mission_EDGERSmission_134_2
            event_target:EDG_ERS_E_purchaser = {
                set_variable = {
                    which = mission_EDGERSmission_82_2_var
                    value = 0
                }
            }
            ai_chance = { 
                factor = 0
            }
        }
    }

                        subtract_variable = { #将西方的国库减去西方乘了0.7的年收入的资金但不超过上限          
                            which = EDG_ERS_E_add_treasury
                            value = 1
                        }
                        add_treasury = 1
                    }
                    set_variable = {
                        which = mission_EDGERSmission_132_6_var
                        value = 0
                    }
                }
            }
            ai_chance = { 
                factor = 100
            }
        }
        option = {
            name = mission_EDGERSmission_134_2
            event_target:EDG_ERS_E_purchaser = {
                set_variable = {
                    which = mission_EDGERSmission_132_6_var
                    value = 0
                }
            }
            ai_chance = { 
                factor = 0
            }
        }
    }
}
